<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it"><a href = vnd.unilang:finale.html>finale</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">finālis</i>. The sports sense derived from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:finale.html>finale</a></i>.

***finch.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:finch.html>finch</a> (8545)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">fynche</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">finċ</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*finkiz</i> (compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vink.html>vink</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Fink</i>), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*(s)pingos</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">chaffinch</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Welsh_language" class="extiw" title="w:Welsh language">Welsh</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="cy">pinc</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:finch.html>finch</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">σπίγγος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">spíngos</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">chaffinch</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Russian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Russian language">Russian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пе́нка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pénka</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:wren.html>wren</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sanskrit" class="extiw" title="w:Sanskrit">Sanskrit</a></span> <i class="Deva mention" lang="sa">फिङ्गक</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="sa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">phiṅgaka</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">drongo, <a href = vnd.unilang:shrike.html>shrike</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:finch.html>finch</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:finches.html>finches</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Any bird of the family Fringillidae, seed-eating passerine <a href = vnd.unilang:birds.html>birds</a>, native chiefly to the Northern Hemisphere and usually having a conical beak.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:finch.html>finch</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:finches.html>finches</a></b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">finching</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">finched</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>To hunt for <a href = vnd.unilang:finches.html>finches</a>, to go finching.</li></ol>

***finnen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:finnen.html>finnen</a> (45516)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Saxon" class="extiw" title="w:Old Saxon">Old Saxon</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="osx">findan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*finþan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*finþaną</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*pent-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to go, pass; path, bridge</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vinden.html>vinden</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">finden</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">find</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">fine</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">finde</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nds"><a href = vnd.unilang:finnen.html>finnen</a></strong> (<i>past singular</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nds">funn</b>, <i>past participle</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nds">funnen</b>, <i>auxiliary verb</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nds"><a href = vnd.unilang:hebben.html>hebben</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to find</li></ol>

***finster.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:finster.html>finster</a> (70120)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle High German">Middle High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh">vinster</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">finstar</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*finistraz</i>, alteration (with the dental and labial articulations switching their positions) of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*þimistraz</i>. From the <i>þ</i>-form also <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">thinstar</i> (<span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle High German">Middle High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh">dinster</i>), <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*thimister</i> (<span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">deemster</i>); from the <i>f</i>-form <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">finistre</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Saxon" class="extiw" title="w:Old Saxon">Old Saxon</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="osx">finistar</i>. Related with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">dämmern</i>. Perhaps also related with Proto-Germanic <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*þiustrijaz</i>, whence German <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">düster</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:duster.html>duster</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:finster.html>finster</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-de comparative-form-of" lang="de">finsterer</b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-de superlative-form-of" lang="de">am finstersten</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">dark</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">gloomy</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">lowering</span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="de">dunkel</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="de">düster</span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> fir (13099)</h1><br><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

***firmament.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:firmament.html>firmament</a> (54522)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:firmament.html>firmament</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">firmāmentum</i>, coined by <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Jerome" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Jerome">Jerome</a> in the Vulgate to render <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">στερέωμα</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">steréōma</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">firm or solid structure</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, which in turn translates <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hebrew_language" class="extiw" title="w:Hebrew language">Hebrew</a></span> <i class="Hebr mention" lang="he">רקיע</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">vault of heaven</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:firmament.html>firmament</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:firmament.html>firmamenten</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:firmament.html>firmament</a></span> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">vault or sphere of the heavens, seen as a solid object in older cosmologies; sky</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">gespan</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">hemelgespan</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uitspansel.html>uitspansel</a></span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr />

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:firmament.html>firmament</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic"><a href = vnd.unilang:o.html>o</a></span>

<ol><li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:formeel.html>formeel</a>)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:hemel.html>hemel</a></li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:fis.html>fis</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">v</span>/<span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>

<dl><dd><ul><li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:toon.html>toon</a> “<b><a href = vnd.unilang:fis.html>fis</a></b>” <a href = vnd.unilang:klinkt.html>klinkt</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> getempereerde <a href = vnd.unilang:stemming.html>stemming</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gelijk.html>gelijk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tonen.html>tonen</a> “eïsis” <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> “ges”.</i> </li></ul></dd></dl></li>

***fishy.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:fishy.html>fishy</a> (65173)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/da/Close_up_of_face_of_young_boy_holds_a_small_fish_in_hand.jpg/170px-Close_up_of_face_of_young_boy_holds_a_small_fish_in_hand.jpg" decoding="async" width="170" height="255" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/da/Close_up_of_face_of_young_boy_holds_a_small_fish_in_hand.jpg/255px-Close_up_of_face_of_young_boy_holds_a_small_fish_in_hand.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/da/Close_up_of_face_of_young_boy_holds_a_small_fish_in_hand.jpg/340px-Close_up_of_face_of_young_boy_holds_a_small_fish_in_hand.jpg 2x" data-file-width="2336" data-file-height="3504" />  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"></div>A boy holding a “fishy” (small fish) in his hand</div></div></div>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">fishi</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">fischey</i>, equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">fish</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">-y</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:fishy.html>fishy</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">fishies</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">childish</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">Diminutive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Latn mention" lang="en">fish</i></span></span>.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1846</b>,  “<span style="font-style: normal;">[</span>Lullabies.<span style="font-style: normal;">]</span> CCLXXVIII.  | <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/When_the_Boat_Comes_In_(song)" class="extiw" title="w:When the Boat Comes In (song)">When the Boat <a href = vnd.unilang:comes.html>Comes</a> In</a>. | ”, in <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/James_Halliwell-Phillipps" class="extiw" title="w:James Halliwell-Phillipps">James Orchard Halliwell</a>, editor, <cite>The Nursery Rhymes of England, Collected Chiefly from Oral Tradition</cite>, 4th edition, London |  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/John_Russell_Smith" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:John Russell Smith">John Russell Smith</a>, 4, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Compton_Street" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Old Compton Street">Old Compton Street</a>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Soho_Square" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Soho Square">Soho Square</a>, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/OCLC" class="extiw" title="w:OCLC">OCLC</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://worldcat.org/oclc/460602989">460602989</a></small>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://books.google.com/books?id=7CkEAAAAQAAJamp;pg=PA133">page 133</a>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">You shall have a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:fishy.html>fishy</a></b> / In a little dishy; / You shall have a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:fishy.html>fishy</a></b> / When the boat <a href = vnd.unilang:comes.html>comes</a> in.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2013</b>,  April V. Costa,  <cite>Fishies and Froggies in the Drain</cite>, Bloomington, Ind. |  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/AuthorHouse" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:AuthorHouse">AuthorHouse</a>, <small>→ISBN</small>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">When Sachie got out of the tub and got her <a href = vnd.unilang:baby.html>baby</a> out of the tub her mom <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> her talk down the drain to the <b>fishies</b> and froggies. <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span> "Are you ready <b>fishies</b>? Are you ready froggies?" Both Sachie and mommy asked together. "One, two, three" they pulled out the plug. And they watched the water go down the drain.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2014</b> May 19,  Patricia <a href = vnd.unilang:averill.html>Averill</a>,  “I Wish I <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> a Little—: Open Ended Songs”, in  <cite>Camp <a href = vnd.unilang:songs.html>Songs</a>, Folk <a href = vnd.unilang:songs.html>Songs</a></cite>, [Bloomington, Ind.] |  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Xlibris" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Xlibris">Xlibris</a>, <small>→ISBN</small>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://books.google.com/books?id=-6S8AwAAQBAJamp;pg=PA304">page 304</a>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">I wish I <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:fishy.html>fishy</a></b> in the sea— / I wish I <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:fishy.html>fishy</a></b> in the sea— / I'd go swimming in the nudie without my bathing suity / <a href = vnd.unilang:oh.html>Oh</a>, I wish I <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:fishy.html>fishy</a></b> in the sea—</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:fishy.html>fishy</a> wishy</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:fishy.html>fishy</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en comparative-form-of" lang="en">fishier</b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en superlative-form-of" lang="en">fishiest</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Of, from, or similar to fish.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">What <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> that <b><a href = vnd.unilang:fishy.html>fishy</a></b> odor?</i></div></dd></dl>

***fixer.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:fixer.html>fixer</a> (83541)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Latn mention" lang="en">fix</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:dictatoriaal.html>-er</a></i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:fixer.html>fixer</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">fixers</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:agent.html>Agent</a> noun of fix; one who, or that which, fixes.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">photography</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A chemical (sodium thiosulfate) used in photographic development that fixes the image in place, preventing further chemical reactions.
<ul><li><b>2003</b>, Bruce <a href = vnd.unilang:warren.html>Warren</a>, <i>Photography: The Concise Guide</i>, Cengage Learning (→ISBN), page 69
<dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">The <b><a href = vnd.unilang:fixer.html>fixer</a></b> removes the undeveloped silver salts from the <a href = vnd.unilang:film.html>film</a>, rendering it no longer sensitive to light. Pour the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:fixer.html>fixer</a></b> — at a temperature within plus or minus 5° F of the developer's — into the tank, using the amount specified by the tank  directions. Agitate with ten inversions initially and then for 10 <a href = vnd.unilang:seconds.html>seconds</a> out of every minute for the remainder of the fixing time. The fixing time <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> not as critical as the developing lime, but stay within the time range suggested in the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:fixer.html>fixer</a></b> directions.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">criminal justice<span class="ib-comma">,</span> law</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A person who arranges immunity for defendants by tampering with the justice system <a href = vnd.unilang:via.html>via</a> bribery or extortion, especially as a business endeavor for profit.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1937</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Edwin_Sutherland" class="extiw" title="w:Edwin Sutherland">Sutherland, Edwin H. (ed)</a> |  Conwell, <a href = vnd.unilang:chic.html>Chic</a> (pseudonym),  <cite>The Professional Thief: by a Professional Thief. Annotated and Interpreted by Edwin H. Sutherland</cite>, Chicago |  University of Chicago Press, <small>LCCN 37036112</small>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">A professional bank robber commented on this [a point in the thief's memoir]: 'Perhaps the author means by this that the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:fixer.html>fixer</a></b> with whom he <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> acquainted works only on crimes not involving violence. It <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> true that there are specialists <a href = vnd.unilang:even.html>even</a> in the fix line, and a <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a> who <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> an in [in = advantageous position] to fix con <a href = vnd.unilang:cases.html>cases</a> might not be able to fix robbery <a href = vnd.unilang:cases.html>cases</a>. But if the author means that the fix does not exist in armed robbery, he <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> badly mistaken. It <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> merely a matter of knowing the right party to go to.'</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">journalism</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A person who <a href = vnd.unilang:assists.html>assists</a> foreign journalists in volatile countries, often providing interpretation, personal connections, and transportation services.
<ul><li><b>2007</b>, Myriam Salama-Carr, <i>Translating and Interpreting Conflict</i>, Rodopi (→ISBN), page 25
<dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Yet at the same time, this <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> also the source of what journalists see as one of the major <a href = vnd.unilang:risks.html>risks</a> involved in dependence on the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:fixer.html>fixer</a></b>: the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:fixer.html>fixer</a></b> may determine, to some  extent, what the journalist <a href = vnd.unilang:sees.html>sees</a>. It <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> at this point that differences between journalists become apparent in the <a href = vnd.unilang:interviews.html>interviews</a> – they give different evaluations of the <a href = vnd.unilang:risks.html>risks</a>. Clearly, this <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a point of tension in their understanding of the situation: the prime positive qualities of the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:fixer.html>fixer</a></b> are also the potentially negative <a href = vnd.unilang:ones.html>ones</a>.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">real estate<span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/United_States" class="extiw" title="w:United States">US</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A fixer-upper.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">the fix <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> in</span></li></ul>

<dl><dd>«<a href = vnd.unilang:nico.html>Nico</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nous.html>nous</a> a <b>fixé</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:des.html>des</a> consos gratos.»
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:nico.html>Nico</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:heeft.html>heeft</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gratis.html>gratis</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:drankjes.html>drankjes</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ons.html>ons</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:geregeld.html>geregeld</a>.</i></dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:fixeren.html>fixeren</a> (57550)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:fixeren.html>fixeren</a></i>, borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm"><a href = vnd.unilang:fixer.html>fixer</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">*<a href = vnd.unilang:fixer.html>fixer</a></i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro"><a href = vnd.unilang:fixen.html>fixe</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">fastened; fixed</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">fīxus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">immovable; steady; stable; fixed</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">fīgere</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to drive in; stick; fasten</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*dʰeygʷ-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to jab; stick; set</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.  Doublet of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:fixen.html>fixen</a></i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:fiksen.html>fiksen</a></i>.
</p>

***fizz.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:fizz.html>fizz</a> (57549)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Onomatopoeia.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:fizz.html>fizz</a></strong> (<i>countable and uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">fizzes</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>An emission of a rapid stream of <a href = vnd.unilang:bubbles.html>bubbles</a>.
<dl><dd><i>I poured a <a href = vnd.unilang:cola.html>cola</a> and waited for the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:fizz.html>fizz</a></b> to settle down before topping off the glass.</i></dd></dl></li>
<li>The sound of such an emission.
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:evan.html>Evan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:sat.html>sat</a> back in the hot tub and listened to the relaxing <b><a href = vnd.unilang:fizz.html>fizz</a></b> and <a href = vnd.unilang:pops.html>pops</a> produced by the eruption of <a href = vnd.unilang:bubbles.html>bubbles</a>. </i></dd></dl></li>
<li>A carbonated beverage, especially <a href = vnd.unilang:champagne.html>champagne</a>.
<dl><dd><i>Nathan ordered an orange <b><a href = vnd.unilang:fizz.html>fizz</a></b> from the soda jerk at the counter.</i></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">emission of <a href = vnd.unilang:bubbles.html>bubbles</a></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">effervescence</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">foam</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">froth</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">head</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">sound of <a href = vnd.unilang:bubbles.html>bubbles</a></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">bubble</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">fizzle</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">hiss</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:sputter.html>sputter</a></span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">carbonated beverage</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">pop</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:seltzer.html>seltzer</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">soda</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:tonic.html>tonic</a></span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:fizz.html>fizz</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">fizzes</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">fizzing</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">fizzed</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To emit <a href = vnd.unilang:bubbles.html>bubbles</a>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To make a rapid hissing or bubbling sound.
<dl><dd><i>the <b>fizzing</b> fuse of a bomb</i></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To shoot or project something moving at great velocity.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2011</b> January 15,  Saj Chowdhury,  “Man City 4 <a href = vnd.unilang:halal.html>-</a> 3 Wolves”, in  <cite>BBC</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/sport2/hi/football/eng_prem/9357962.stm">[1]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">And just before the interval, Kolarov, who <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> having one of his better games in a City <a href = vnd.unilang:shirt.html>shirt</a>, <b>fizzed</b> in a cracker from 30 <a href = vnd.unilang:yards.html>yards</a> which the <a href = vnd.unilang:wolves.html>Wolves</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:stopper.html>stopper</a> unconvincingly <a href = vnd.unilang:pushed.html>pushed</a> behind for a corner.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li>To travel at a great velocity, producing a sound caused by the speed.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2011</b> January 15,  <a href = vnd.unilang:sam.html>Sam</a> Sheringham,  “Chelsea 2 -03 Blackburn Rovers”, in  <cite>BBC</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/sport2/hi/football/eng_prem/9358426.stm">[2]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:terry.html>Terry</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:came.html>came</a> close to doubling Chelsea's lead when his header from Lampard's mis-hit <a href = vnd.unilang:volley.html>volley</a> fizzed <a href = vnd.unilang:inches.html>inches</a> past the upright.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms_2">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">emit <a href = vnd.unilang:bubbles.html>bubbles</a></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">bubble</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">effervesce</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">foam</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">froth</span></li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:fladderen.html>fladderen</a> (31241)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Related to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">vleder</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">wing</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">fledarôn</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*fleþarô</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">wing</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, probably related to <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*fifaldǭ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">butterfly</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. See also <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">flattern</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to flutter</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Falter</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">moth</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<p><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> missing or incomplete. Please add to it, or discuss it at the Etymology scriptorium.)</span>

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:flansen.html>flansen</a></strong>
</p>

<p>In contemporary Dutch this verb usually requires the prepositional phrases <i><a href = vnd.unilang:aaneen.html>aaneen</a></i> or <i>in <a href = vnd.unilang:elkaar.html>elkaar</a></i>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:flapdrol.html>flapdrol</a> (21642)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">flap</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">flap, loose-hanging cloth</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:drol.html>drol</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">fool</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. First attested in the mid 19th century.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:flapdrol.html>flapdrol</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:flapdrollen.html>flapdrollen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:flapdrol.html>flapdrolletje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informal<span class="ib-comma">,</span> mildly derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> fool, nincompoop.
<ul><li><b>1850</b> October 24, "<a href = vnd.unilang:gemengde.html>Gemengde</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:berichten.html>berichten</a>", <i>Zierikzeesche Nieuwsbode</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:vol.html>vol</a>. 7, issue 705, page 2.
